51 - Select s1, s2, s3 such that ParentStar(s1, _) and ParentStar(s2, s3)
stmt s1, s2, s3, s4; prog_line e1, e2, e3, e4; procedure p1, p2, p3, p4; assign a1, a2, a3, a4; if if1, if2, if3, if4; while w1, w2, w3, w4; call o1, o2, o3, o4; variable v1, v2, v3, v4; constant c1, c2, c3, c4;
Select <s1, s2, s3> such that Parent*(s1, _) and Parent*(s2, s3)

69 - Select s2, p2 such that FollowsStar(a1, s1) and Affects(s1, s2) CallsStar(p2, p3) anud Uses(p2, v)
stmt s1, s2, s3, s4; prog_line e1, e2, e3, e4; procedure p1, p2, p3, p4; assign a1, a2, a3, a4; if if1, if2, if3, if4; while w1, w2, w3, w4; call o1, o2, o3, o4; variable v1, v2, v3, v4; constant c1, c2, c3, c4;
Select <a1, s1, s2> such that Follows*(a1, s1) and Affects(s1, s2) and Calls*(p2, p3) and Uses(p2, "i")
